<table style="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt;border:0;width:100%" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0">
<tr style="page-break-inside:avoid">
<td style="width:11%;vertical-align:top" align="left"><span style="font-weight:bold">Item&#8201;2.02.</span></td>
<td align="left" style="vertical-align:top"> <p style=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;text-align:left">Results of Operations and Financial Condition. </p></td></tr></table> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On October&#160;24, 2024, we issued the press release furnished as Exhibit 99.1. The press release describes the results of our operations for the quarter ended September&#160;30, 2024. </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The information furnished in this Current Report on Form <span style="white-space:nowrap">8-K</span> under Item 2.02 and the attached exhibit shall not be deemed &#8220;filed&#8221; for purposes of Section&#160;18 of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as amended (the &#8220;Exchange Act&#8221;), or incorporated by reference in any filing under the Securities Act of 1933, as amended, or the Exchange Act, except as shall be expressly set forth by specific reference in such a filing. </p> <p style="font-size:18pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&#160;</p>
<table style="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt;border:0;width:100%" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0">
<tr style="page-break-inside:avoid">
<td style="width:11%;vertical-align:top" align="left"><span style="font-weight:bold">Item&#8201;8.01.</span></td>
<td align="left" style="vertical-align:top"> <p style=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;text-align:left">Other Events. </p></td></tr></table> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On October&#160;24, 2024, we announced that our board of directors declared a quarterly cash dividend of US $0.53 per share. The dividend will have a record date of November&#160;7, 2024, payable on December&#160;12, 2024. The dividend will be paid in U.S. currency to holders of ResMed&#8217;s common stock trading on the New York Stock Exchange. Holders of CHESS Depositary Instruments trading on the Australian Securities Exchange will receive an equivalent amount in Australian currency, based on the exchange rate on the record date, and reflecting the 10:1 ratio between CDIs and NYSE shares. The <span style="white-space:nowrap">ex-dividend</span> date will be November&#160;6, 2024, for common stockholders and for CDI holders. ResMed has received a waiver from the ASX&#8217;s settlement operating rules, which will allow ResMed to defer processing conversions between its common stock and CDI registers from November&#160;6, 2024, through November&#160;7, 2024, inclusive.</p> <p style="font-size:18pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&#160;</p>

<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><I>Year-over-year revenue grows 11%, operating profit up
34%,</I><I></I><I><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">&nbsp;non-GAAP</FONT></I><I></I><I>&nbsp;operating profit up 27%</I> </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><I>Operating cash flow of $326&nbsp;million</I> </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>Note: A webcast of ResMed&#146;s conference call will be available at 4:30 p.m. ET today at</I>&nbsp;<I><U>http://investor.resmed.com</U></I> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">SAN DIEGO, October&nbsp;24, 2024 &#150; ResMed Inc. (NYSE: RMD, ASX: RMD) today announced results for its quarter ended September&nbsp;30, 2024. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>First Quarter 2025 Highlights </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>All comparisons are to
the prior year period</I> </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Revenue increased by 11% to $1.2&nbsp;billion; up 11% on a constant currency basis</P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

improved 320 bps to 59.2% </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

operations up 27% </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

per share of $2.20 </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;Our first-quarter fiscal year 2025 results reflect ongoing momentum and strong execution across all areas of
our business,&#148; said Mick Farrell, Chairman and CEO of ResMed. &#147;We delivered 11% year-over-year revenue growth, and our focus on operational excellence resulted in another quarter of year-over-year margin expansion and a 34% increase in
operating profit. As we celebrate 35 years of growth and innovation, our recently launched 2030 strategy will further enable us to transform sleep health, breathing health, and healthcare technology at home. By building on our leadership in
connected digital health, we are driving better care, simplifying the health journey, and improving access to our therapies globally so even more people worldwide are empowered to live healthier, higher-quality lives using products and services they
love.&#148; </P>

foreign currency fluctuations, we provide certain financial information on a &#147;constant currency&#148; basis, which is in addition to the actual financial information presented. In order to calculate our constant currency information, we
translate the current period financial information using the foreign currency exchange rates that were in effect during the previous comparable period. However, constant currency measures should not be considered in isolation or as an alternative to
U.S. dollar measures that reflect current period exchange rates, or to other financial measures calculated and presented in accordance with U.S. GAAP. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

increase in SG&amp;A expenses was mainly due to increases in employee-related expenses. SG&amp;A expenses improved to 19.5&nbsp;percent of revenue in the quarter, compared with 20.2&nbsp;percent in the same period of the prior year.

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Net income for the quarter was $311&nbsp;million and diluted earnings per share was <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">$2.11.&nbsp;Non-GAAP&nbsp;net</FONT> income increased by 35&nbsp;percent to $325&nbsp;million, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">and&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;diluted</FONT> earnings per share increased by 34&nbsp;percent to
$2.20, predominantly attributable to strong sales growth and gross margin improvement. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

$50&nbsp;million as part of our ongoing capital management. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Other Business and Operational Highlights </I></B></P>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Celebrated 35 years of innovation and 25 years listed on the New York Stock Exchange (NYSE) by ringing the
Opening Bell<SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">&reg;</SUP> at the NYSE on its listing anniversary. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Held its 2024 Investor Day and unveiled ResMed&#146;s 2030 strategy to drive growth, profitability, and
shareholder returns. As part of Investor Day, announced five-year revenue and earnings growth outlook, supported by ResMed&#146;s plans to accelerate product and technology innovation, operational excellence, commercial execution, and financial
strength. ResMed&#146;s updated ambition is to help more than 500&nbsp;million people achieve their full health potential in 2030. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">ResMed operates two reporting units, historically named &#145;Sleep and Respiratory Care&#146; and
&#145;SaaS&#146;. In alignment with the 2030 Strategy announced during Investor Day in September, these reporting units have been renamed to Sleep and Breathing Health (formerly Sleep and Respiratory Care) and Residential Care Software (formerly
SaaS). The methodology for attributing financial results to these reporting units remains unchanged. Revenue from prior periods is consistent and comparable to previous reporting. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Announced the upcoming launch of ResMed&#146;s first fabric mask, the AirTouch N30i. With a fabric-wrapped frame
featuring a soft, breathable, and moisture wicking design, the AirTouch N30i is designed to create a more natural and comfortable experience for users making it even easier to embrace CPAP therapy. AirTouch N30i will be available in the U.S.
beginning next week. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Introduced several new patient-centric products encompassing digital and personalized solutions to enhance the
therapy journey for sleep apnea patients. The innovations integrate with digital wearable devices and incorporate generative artificial intelligence to deliver a more personalized sleep health experience. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Dividend program </I></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The ResMed board of directors
today declared a quarterly cash dividend of $0.53 per share. The dividend will have a record date of November&nbsp;7, 2024, payable on December&nbsp;12, 2024. The dividend will be paid in U.S. currency to holders of ResMed&#146;s common stock
trading on the New York Stock Exchange. Holders of CHESS Depositary Interests (&#147;CDIs&#148;) trading on the Australian Securities Exchange will receive an equivalent amount in Australian currency, based on the exchange rate on the record date,
and reflecting the 10:1 ratio between CDIs and NYSE shares. <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">The&nbsp;ex-dividend&nbsp;date</FONT> will be November&nbsp;6, 2024, for common stockholders and for CDI holders. ResMed has received a waiver from the
ASX&#146;s settlement operating rules, which will allow ResMed to defer processing conversions between its common stock and CDI registers from November&nbsp;6, 2024, through November&nbsp;7, 2024, inclusive.</P>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Webcast details </I></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">ResMed will discuss its first quarter fiscal year 2025 results on its webcast at 1:30 p.m. U.S. Pacific Time today. The live webcast of the call can be
accessed on ResMed&#146;s Investor Relations website at <U>investor.resmed.com.</U> Please go to this section of the website and click on the icon for the &#147;Q1 2025 Earnings Webcast&#148; to register and listen to the live webcast. A replay of
the earnings webcast will be accessible on the website and available approximately two hours after the live webcast. In addition, a telephone replay of the conference call will be available approximately three hours after the webcast by dialing <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">+1&nbsp;877-660-6853&nbsp;(U.S.)</FONT></FONT> or <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">+1&nbsp;201-612-7415&nbsp;(outside</FONT></FONT> U.S.) and entering the
passcode 13749420. The telephone replay will be available until November&nbsp;7, 2024. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>About ResMed </I></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">At ResMed (NYSE: RMD, ASX: RMD) we pioneer innovative solutions that treat and keep people out of the hospital, empowering them to live healthier,
higher-quality lives. Our digital health technologies and cloud-connected medical devices transform care for people with sleep apnea, COPD, and other chronic diseases. Our
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">comprehensive&nbsp;out-of-hospital&nbsp;software</FONT></FONT> platforms support the professionals and caregivers who help people stay healthy in the home or care setting of their
choice. By enabling better care, we improve quality of life, reduce the impact of chronic disease, and lower costs for consumers and healthcare systems in more than 140 countries.&nbsp;To learn more, visit <U>ResMed.com</U> and follow @ResMed. </P>

<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(A)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">ResMed adjusts for the impact of the amortization of acquired intangibles, field safety notification expenses,
acquisition related expenses and associated tax effects from their evaluation of ongoing operations, and believes that investors benefit from adjusting these items to facilitate a more meaningful evaluation of current operating performance.
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">ResMed believes <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">that&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;diluted</FONT> earnings per share is an
additional measure of performance that investors can use to compare operating results between reporting periods. ResMed <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">uses&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;information</FONT> internally in planning, forecasting, and evaluating
the results of operations in the current period and in comparing it to past periods. ResMed believes this information provides investors better insight when evaluating ResMed&#146;s performance from core operations and provides consistent financial
reporting. The use <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">of&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;measures</FONT> is intended to supplement, and not to replace, the presentation of net income and other GAAP measures. Like <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">all&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;measures,&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;earnings</FONT></FONT> are subject to inherent limitations because they do not include all the expenses that must be included under GAAP. </P>

<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(B)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">In order to provide a framework for assessing how our underlying businesses performed excluding the effect of
foreign currency fluctuations, we provide certain financial information on a &#147;constant currency basis,&#148; which is in addition to the actual financial information presented. In order to calculate our constant currency information, we
translate the current period financial information using the foreign currency exchange rates that were in effect during the previous comparable period. However, constant currency measures should not be considered in isolation or as an alternative to
U.S. dollar measures that reflect current period exchange rates, or to other financial measures calculated and presented in accordance with U.S. GAAP. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
